				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Musikalisches Opfer, BWV 1079 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>13, in 3 chapters
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1747
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Fugues&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Fugues</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sonatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sonatas</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Musikalisches Opfer
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Musical Offering
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 1079&#160;; Op.6
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 408
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>13 pieces, in 3 chapters
<dl><dd> <i>Regis issu cantio et reliqua canonica arte resoluta</i>
<ul><li> Ricercar a 3
</li><li> Ricercar a 6
</li></ul>
</dd><dd> <i>Sonata sopr' il soggetto Reale a traversa, violino e continuo</i>
<dl><dd> I. Largo
</dd><dd> II. Allegro
</dd><dd> III. Andante
</dd><dd> IV. Allegro
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd> <i>Thematis Regii elaborationes canonicae</i>
<ul><li> Canones diversi super Thema Regium
</li></ul>
<dl><dd> 1. Canon a 2 cancrizans
</dd><dd> 2. Canon a 2 violini in unisono
</dd><dd> 3. Canon a 2 per motum contrarium
</dd><dd> 4. Canon a 2 per augmentationem, contrario motu
</dd><dd> 5. Canon a 2 per tonos
</dd><dd> 6. Fuga canonica in epidiapente
</dd><dd> 7. Canon perpetuus super thema Regium
</dd><dd> 8. Canon perpetuus
</dd></dl>
<ul><li> Quaerendo invenietis
</li></ul>
<dl><dd> 9. Canon a 2 
</dd><dd> 10. Canon a 4
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1747
</td></tr>
